When compaction aborts and retries, the counter increments but the session context stays the same, causing the same content to be flushed repeatedly (4-7x duplicate entries reported).\\n\\nRoot cause: `compactionCount` conflates \\u0026#34;compaction cycle count\\u0026#34; with \\u0026#34;content has changed\\u0026#34; — these are independent concerns. Two different compaction cycles can see identical context (abort → retry scenario), so event-based dedup is fundamentally wrong for this use case.\\n\\n## How\\n- **State-based dedup**: compute a SHA-256 hash (truncated to 16 hex chars) of `messages.length + last 3 user/assistant message contents` before each flush. If the hash matches the stored `memoryFlushContextHash`, skip the flush.\\n- **Two-layer design**: `shouldRunMemoryFlush()` unchanged (token threshold gate), hash check added as second gate in `runMemoryFlushIfNeeded()`.\\n- **`willRetry` fix**: `onAgentEvent` now checks `!evt.data?.willRetry` before marking `memoryCompactionCompleted = true`, preventing retry-in-progress compaction from being incorrectly treated as completed.\\n- **Performance**: `readTranscriptTailMessages()` reads only the last 64KB of the transcript file (not the full file).\\n- **Hash timing**: stores the hash computed *before* the flush run (not after), since the flush turn itself writes to the transcript and would change the hash.\\n\\n### Scenario behavior\\n| Scenario | Behavior |\\n|----------|----------|\\n| Compaction abort | messages unchanged → hash unchanged → skip ✅ |\\n| Compaction success | messages compressed → hash changed → allow flush ✅ |\\n| New messages | tail content changed → hash changed → allow flush ✅ |\\n| Persistence failure | `contextHashBeforeFlush` used in-memory → no re-flush within session ✅ |\\n\\n## Files changed (3 + 1 test)\\n- `src/auto-reply/reply/memory-flush.ts` — new `computeContextHash()` function\\n- `src/auto-reply/reply/agent-runner-memory.ts` — hash check gate + willRetry fix + tail reader\\n- `src/config/sessions/types.ts` — add `memoryFlushContextHash` field to `SessionEntry`\\n- `src/auto-reply/reply/memory-flush.test.ts` — 8 unit tests for `computeContextHash`\\n\\n## Testing\\n- [x] `pnpm build` passes\\n- [x] `pnpm check` passes (lint + format)\\n- [x] `pnpm test` — 811/812 pass (1 pre-existing failure in `process-respawn.test.ts`)\\n- [x] 8 new unit tests for `computeContextHash` (empty input, object content, undefined content, system message filtering, length differentiation, tail behavior)\\n- [x] AI-assisted (OpenClaw agents 李飞飞/陈皮皮/毛豆豆, cross-reviewed, fully tested)\\n\\n## Backward compatibility\\n- `memoryFlushContextHash` undefined → falls back to existing `compactionCount` logic\\n- `memoryFlushCompactionCount` field preserved (not removed)\\n-
